### You've made friends with another child in the court ###
character_event = {
	id = friends_rivals.200

	min_age = 4
	max_age = 14
	prisoner = no
	capable_only = yes
	
	hide_window = yes
	lacks_dlc = "Conclave"
	
	trigger = {
		#NOT = { num_of_friends = 2 }
		#NOT = { num_of_rivals = 2 }
		NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
		NOT = { trait = dragon }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 80
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_primary_heir = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = gregarious
		}	
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = shy
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_abroad = no
				prisoner = no
				at_location = ROOT
				NOT = { trait = dragon }
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				NOT = { character = ROOT }
				same_sex = ROOT
				NOT = { trait = craven }
				NOT = { trait = honest }
				NOT = { sibling = ROOT }
				age = 4
				NOT = { age = 14 }
				#NOT = {num_of_friends = 2}
				#NOT = {num_of_rivals = 2}
				NOT = { is_friend = ROOT }
				NOT = { is_rival = ROOT }
			}	
			character_event = { id = friends_rivals.201 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}	
character_event = {
	id = friends_rivals.201

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROM = { character_event = { id = 100000 } }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}	
character_event = {
	id = 100000
	desc = EVTDESC100000
	picture = GFX_evt_child_sword
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100000
		FROM = {
			add_rival = ROOT
			character_event = {
				id = 100001
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100001
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB100000
		FROM = {
			add_friend = ROOT
			character_event = {
				id = 100002
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100002
			}
		}
	}
}

#New rival is notified
character_event = {
	id = 100001
	desc = EVTDESC100001
	picture = GFX_evt_child_sword
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100001
		add_rival = FROM
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { personality_traits = 5 }
				NOT = { trait = wroth }
				NOT = { trait = patient }
				trait = greedy
			}
			add_trait = wroth
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { personality_traits = 5 }
				NOT = { trait = greedy }
				NOT = { trait = charitable }
				trait = wroth
			}
			add_trait = greedy
		}
	}
}

#New friend is notified
character_event = {
	id = 100002
	desc = EVTDESC100002
	picture = GFX_evt_child_sword
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100002
		add_friend = FROM
	}
}

### One of the other children in court is very shy and would rather read than play with us ###
character_event = {
	id = friends_rivals.202

	min_age = 4
	max_age = 14
	prisoner = no
	capable_only = yes
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	trigger = {
		#NOT = {num_of_friends = 2}
		#NOT = {num_of_rivals = 2}
		OR = {
			trait = gregarious
			trait = charitable
			trait = brave
		}
		NOT = { trait = dragon }
		NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 80
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = cruel
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				at_location = ROOT
				NOT = { character = ROOT }
				NOT = { trait = dragon }
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				prisoner = no
				age = 4
				NOT = {
					age = 14
				}
				NOT = {
					is_friend = ROOT
				}
				NOT = {
					is_rival = ROOT
				}
				#NOT = {num_of_friends = 2}
				#NOT = {num_of_rivals = 2}
				NOT = {
					sibling = ROOT
				}
				trait = shy
				NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
			}	
			character_event = { id = friends_rivals.203 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}	
character_event = {
	id = friends_rivals.203

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROM = { character_event = { id = 100005 } }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}	
character_event = {
	id = 100005
	desc = EVTDESC100005
	picture = GFX_evt_child_talking
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
		
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100005
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = cruel
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = ruthless
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = greedy
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = 100006
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100006
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB100005
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = kind
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = honorable
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = charitable
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = gregarious
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = 100007
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100007
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC100005
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				trait = gregarious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				trait = charitable
			}
		}
		prestige = 5
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = charitable }
				trait = gregarious
			}
			remove_trait = gregarious
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = gregarious }
				trait = charitable
			}
			remove_trait = charitable
		}
	}
}

#Kick his butt or ignore him?
character_event = {
	id = 100006
	desc = EVTDESC100006
	picture = GFX_evt_child_bully
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100006
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = brave
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.01
				trait = craven
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = proud
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = 100008
				days = 1
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100008
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB100006
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.01
				trait = brave
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = craven
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = patient
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = humble
			}
		}
		add_trait = stressed
	}
}

#Borrow FROM's sword?
character_event = {
	id = 100007
	desc = EVTDESC100007
	picture = GFX_evt_child_talking
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100007
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = brave
			}
		}
		add_friend = FROM
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = 100012
				days = 1
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100012
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB100007
		trigger = { NOT = { trait = brave } NOT = { trait = berserker } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = craven
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { personality_traits = 5 }
				NOT = { trait = craven }
				NOT = { trait = brave }
			}
			add_trait = craven
		}
	}
}

### My guardian was ready to rip me a new one when someone interfered ###
character_event = {
	id = friends_rivals.204

	min_age = 6
	max_age = 16
	prisoner = no
	capable_only = yes
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_guardian = yes
		trait = slothful
		NOT = { trait = dragon }
		#NOT = {num_of_friends = 2}
		#NOT = {num_of_rivals = 2}
		NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 80
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = wroth
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = dragon }
				NOT = { character = ROOT }
				age = 6
				NOT = { age = 16 }
				same_guardian = ROOT
				NOT = { sibling = ROOT }
				OR = {
					trait = charitable
					trait = kind
					trait = ambitious
				}
				#NOT = {num_of_friends = 3}
				#NOT = {num_of_rivals = 3}
				NOT = {
					is_friend = ROOT
				}
				NOT = {
					is_rival = ROOT
				}
			}	
			character_event = { id = friends_rivals.205 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}	
character_event = {
	id = friends_rivals.205

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROM = { character_event = { id = 100015 } }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}	
character_event = {
	id = 100015
	desc = EVTDESC100015
	picture = GFX_evt_child_bully

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100015
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = patient
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = gregarious
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			add_friend = ROOT
			character_event = {
				id = 100016
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPA100016
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB100015
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = selfish
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_irritated
				who = ROOT
				years = 100
			}
			set_character_flag = wrongly_interfered
			character_event = {
				id = 100016
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPB100016
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC100015
		trigger = { NOT = { trait = deceitful } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = honest
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = honorable
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = just
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { personality_traits = 5 }
				NOT = { trait = honest }
			}
			add_trait = honest
		}
	}
}

#Gain friend/gain rival
character_event = {
	id = 100016
	desc = EVTDESC100016
	picture = GFX_evt_child_bully
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100016
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_character_flag = wrongly_interfered
			}
		}
		add_friend = FROM
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB100016
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = wrongly_interfered
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = ruthless
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = cruel
			}
		}
		clr_character_flag = wrongly_interfered
		add_rival = FROM
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = 100017
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100017
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC100016
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = wrongly_interfered
			NOT = { trait = ambitious }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = patient
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = honorable
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = kind
			}
		}
		clr_character_flag = wrongly_interfered
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { personality_traits = 5 }
				NOT = { trait = content }
			}
			add_trait = content
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTD100016
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = wrongly_interfered
			NOT = { trait = charitable }
			NOT = { trait = familyperson }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = cynical
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = shy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = selfish
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = charitable
			}
		}
		clr_character_flag = wrongly_interfered
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { personality_traits = 5 }
				NOT = { trait = selfish }
			}
			add_trait = selfish
		}
		change_intrigue = 1
	}
}

#Gain rival
character_event = {
	id = 100017
	desc = EVTDESC100017
	picture = GFX_evt_child_bully
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100017
		add_rival = FROM
	}
}
	
### A fellow student lacks even the ability to talk to a girl ###
character_event = {
	id = friends_rivals.206

	only_men = yes
	prisoner = no
	min_age = 14
	max_age = 25
	capable_only = yes
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_married = no
		OR = {
			trait = seducer
			trait = lustful
		}	
		#NOT = {num_of_friends = 5}
		#NOT = {num_of_rivals = 5}
		NOT = { trait = shy }
		NOT = { trait = dragon }
		NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 80
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = cruel
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			trait = seducer
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			has_focus = focus_seduction
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				at_location = ROOT
				#same_liege = ROOT
				#is_female = no
				prisoner = no
				is_married = no
				NOT = { trait = dragon }
				NOT = { character = ROOT }
				age = 14
				NOT = { age = 25 }
				#NOT = {num_of_friends = 5}
				#NOT = {num_of_rivals = 5}
				NOT = {
					sibling = ROOT
				}
				NOT = {
					is_friend = ROOT
				}
				NOT = {
					is_rival = ROOT
				}
				NOT = { trait = gregarious }
				NOT = { trait = seducer }
				has_lover = no
			}	
			character_event = { id = friends_rivals.207 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}	
character_event = {
	id = friends_rivals.207

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROM = { character_event = { id = 100020 } }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}	
character_event = {
	id = 100020
	desc = EVTDESC100020
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100020
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = kind
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = charitable
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = honorable
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = patient
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = 100021
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100021
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB100020
		trigger = { NOT = { trait = charitable } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = cruel
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = greedy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = ruthless
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = wroth
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { personality_traits = 5 }
				NOT = { trait = greedy }
				NOT = { trait = charitable }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				add_trait = greedy
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38252
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Offered help
character_event = {
	id = 100021
	desc = EVTDESC100021
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100021
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = diligent
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = honorable
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = patient
			}
		}
		add_friend = FROM
		if = {
			limit = { trait = shy }
			remove_trait = shy
		}	
		if = {
			limit = { trait = chaste }
			remove_trait = chaste
		}		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = 100022
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100022
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB100021
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = ambitious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = ruthless
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = wroth
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = shy }
			random = {
				chance = 50
				remove_trait = shy
				hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 38295 } }
			}	
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				set_character_flag = help_rejected
				character_event = {
					id = 100023
					tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100023
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC100021
		trigger = { NOT = { trait = humble } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = content
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = slothful
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { personality_traits = 5 }
				NOT = { trait = proud }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 25
				add_trait = proud
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38261 #Notify Shy
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				set_character_flag = help_rejected_politely
				character_event = {
					id = 100023
					tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100023
				}
			}
		}
	}

### Ladies shun me, I need help! ###
character_event = {
	id = friends_rivals.208

	only_men = yes
	prisoner = no
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 25
	capable_only = yes
	war = no
	hide_window = yes
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		is_married = no
		has_lover = no
		NOT = { trait = dragon }
		#NOT = {num_of_friends = 5}
		#NOT = {num_of_rivals = 5}
		OR = {
			trait = paranoid
			trait = shy
		}
		NOT = { trait = depressed }
		NOT = { trait = gregarious }
		NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 80
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = slothful
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = dragon }
				at_location = ROOT
				is_female = no
				war = no
				in_command = no
				prisoner = no
				age = 16
				NOT = {
					age = 25
				}
				NOT = {
					sibling = ROOT
				}
				#NOT = {num_of_friends = 5}
				#NOT = {num_of_rivals = 5}
				trait = lustful
				OR = {
					trait = charitable
					trait = kind
					trait = gregarious
				}
				NOT = {
					is_friend = ROOT
				}
				NOT = {
					is_rival = ROOT
				}
			}	
			character_event = { id = friends_rivals.209 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}

			trait = cynical
		}

	}

				NOT = {
					age = 25
				}
				trait = lustful
				OR = {
					trait = trusting
					trait = charitable
					trait = kind
					trait = gregarious
				}
				NOT = {
					sibling = ROOT
				}
				NOT = {
					is_friend = ROOT
				}
				NOT = {
					is_rival = ROOT
				}

		}

	}
}

character_event = {
	id = friends_rivals.216

	capable_only = yes	
	hide_window = yes	
	min_age = 11
	max_age = 16
	prisoner = no

		NOT = {
			combat_rating = 4
		}
		NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 80
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = craven
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = content
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = dragon }
				combat_rating = 4
				OR = {
					is_female = no
					culture = kayakayanayan
					culture = samyrianan
					culture = bayasabhadi
				}
				age = 11
				NOT = {
					age = 16
				}
				at_location = ROOT
				NOT = {
					sibling = ROOT
				}
				NOT = {
					is_friend = ROOT
				}
				NOT = {
					is_rival = ROOT
				}
			}	
			character_event = { id = friends_rivals.217 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = OK
	}

	max_age = 16
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			trait = cruel
			trait = wroth
			trait = envious
		}
		NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 80
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			intrigue = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { intrigue = 5 }
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = dragon }
				prisoner = no
				same_sex = ROOT
				age = 11
				NOT = {
					age = 16
				}
				at_location = ROOT
				NOT = {
					sibling = ROOT
				}
				NOT = {
					is_friend = ROOT
				}
				NOT = {
					is_rival = ROOT
				}
			}	
			character_event = { id = friends_rivals.221 }
		}
	}

		name = OK
	}

#ROOT tries to convert a cynic
character_event = {
	id = 100081
	desc = EVTDESC100081
	picture = GFX_evt_child_talking
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100081
		add_rival = FROM
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = 100082
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100082
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB100081
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					personality_traits = 5
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = deceitful
				}
			}
			add_trait = deceitful
		}
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = 100083
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100083
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC100081
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					personality_traits = 5
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = zealous
				}
			}
			add_trait = zealous
			hidden_tooltip = { remove_trait = cynical }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					religion = FROM
				}
			}
			religion = FROM
		}
		add_friend = FROM
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = 100084
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100084
			}
		}
	}
}

### My embroidery is not as good as someone elses! ###
character_event = {
	id = friends_rivals.224

	capable_only = yes
	hide_window = yes	
	only_women = yes
	min_age = 11
	max_age = 16
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			trait = ambitious
			trait = diligent
		}
		NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 80
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			trait = envious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = kind
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_female = yes
				age = 6
				NOT = {
					age = 11
				}
				at_location = ROOT
				OR = {
					trait = ambitious
					trait = diligent
				}
				NOT = {
					sibling = ROOT
				}
				NOT = {
					is_friend = ROOT
				}
				NOT = {
					is_rival = ROOT
				}
				NOT = { trait = dragon }
			}	
			character_event = { id = friends_rivals.225 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}

### Someone stole my doll! ###
character_event = {
	id = friends_rivals.226

	capable_only = yes	
	hide_window = yes	
	only_women = yes
	min_age = 4
	max_age = 14
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 80
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = humble
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = envious
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = dragon }
				at_location = ROOT
				is_female = yes
				is_abroad = no
				prisoner = no
				age = 4
				NOT = {
					age = 14
				}
				NOT = {
					sibling = ROOT
				}
				OR = {
					trait = deceitful
					trait = greedy
				}
				NOT = {
					opinion = { who = ROOT value = 10 }
				}
				NOT = {
					is_friend = ROOT
				}
				NOT = {
					is_rival = ROOT
				}
			}	
			character_event = { id = friends_rivals.227 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}	
character_event = {
	id = friends_rivals.227

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROM = { character_event = { id = 100100 } }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}
character_event = {
	id = 100100
	desc = EVTDESC100100
	picture = GFX_evt_child_bully
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100100
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					personality_traits = 5
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = ambitious
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 25
				add_trait = ambitious
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38278 #Notify Ambitious
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					personality_traits = 5
					trait = ambitious
				}
				piety = 5
			}			
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				character_event = {
					id = 100101
					days = 1
					tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100101
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB100100
		random = {
			chance = 20
			add_trait = depressed
			hidden_tooltip = {
				character_event = {
					id = 38288 #Notify Depressed
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Courtier decides what happens to doll
character_event = {
	id = 100101
	desc = EVTDESC100101
	picture = GFX_evt_child_talking
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100101
		add_friend = FROM
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = 100102
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPA100102
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB100101
		tooltip = {
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_grateful
				who = FROM
				years = 5
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			set_character_flag = ugly_doll
			character_event = {
				id = 100102
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPA100102
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC100101
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					personality_traits = 5
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = greedy
				}
			}
			add_trait = greedy
		}
		add_rival = FROM
		FROM = {
			set_character_flag = rival_doll
			character_event = {
				id = 100102
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPB100102
			}
		}
	}
}

#Gave it back
character_event = {
	id = 100102
	desc = EVTDESC100102
	picture = GFX_evt_child_talking
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100102
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_character_flag = ugly_doll
			}
		}
		add_friend = FROM
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB100102
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = ugly_doll
		}
		clr_character_flag = ugly_doll
		opinion = {
			modifier = opinion_grateful
			who = FROM
			years = 5
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC100102
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = rival_doll
		}
		clr_character_flag = rival_doll
		add_rival = FROM
	}
}

### Learn from the best (and take his job) ###
character_event = {
	id = friends_rivals.228
	
	hide_window = yes	
	only_rulers = yes
	min_age = 16
	prisoner = no
	capable_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_councillor = no
		NOT = { is_voter = yes }
		independent = no
		OR = {
			has_ambition = obj_become_chancellor
			has_ambition = obj_become_marshal
			has_ambition = obj_become_treasurer
			has_ambition = obj_become_spymaster
			has_ambition = obj_become_spiritual
			has_ambition = obj_become_castellan
		}
		liege = { NOT = { character = ROOT } }
		NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 80
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_smart_trigger = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = genius
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = diligent
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = content
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		liege = {
			random_courtier = {
				limit = {
					is_councillor = yes
					same_liege = ROOT
					OR = {
						AND = {
							has_job_title = job_chancellor
							ROOT = {
								has_ambition = obj_become_chancellor
							}
						}
						AND = {
							has_job_title = job_marshal
							ROOT = {
								has_ambition = obj_become_marshal
							}
						}
						AND = {
							has_job_title = job_treasurer
							ROOT = {
								has_ambition = obj_become_treasurer
							}
						}
						AND = {
							has_job_title = job_spymaster
							ROOT = {
								has_ambition = obj_become_spymaster
							}
						}
						AND = {
							has_job_title = job_spiritual
							ROOT = {
								has_ambition = obj_become_spiritual
							}
						}
						AND = {
							has_job_title = job_castellan
							ROOT = {
								has_ambition = obj_become_castellan
							}
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						is_friend = ROOT
					}
					NOT = {
						is_rival = ROOT
					}
				}	
				character_event = { id = friends_rivals.229 }
			}
		}	
	}
	
	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}

#Gain friend
character_event = {
	id = 100112
	desc = EVTDESC100112
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100112
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_character_flag = suspicious_chancellor
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					has_job_title = job_chancellor
				}
				has_ambition = obj_become_chancellor
			}
			change_diplomacy = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					has_job_title = job_marshal
				}
				has_ambition = obj_become_marshal
			}
			change_martial = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					has_job_title = job_treasurer
				}
				has_ambition = obj_become_treasurer
			}
			change_stewardship = 1
		}	
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					has_job_title = job_spymaster
				}
				has_ambition = obj_become_spymaster
			}
			change_intrigue = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					has_job_title = job_spiritual
				}
				has_ambition = obj_become_spiritual
			}
			change_learning = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					has_job_title = job_castellan
				}
				has_ambition = obj_become_castellan
			}
			change_stewardship = 1
		}
		add_friend = FROM
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100112
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = suspicious_chancellor
		}
		clr_character_flag = suspicious_chancellor
		tooltip = {
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_glad
				who = FROM
				years = 100
			}
		}
	}
}

### Friend at war - send help? ###
character_event = {
	id = 100150
	desc = EVTDESC100150
	picture = GFX_evt_large_army
	
	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 16
	prisoner = no
	capable_only = yes
	war = no
	friends = yes
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		scaled_wealth = 0.5
		NOT = {
			has_character_modifier = friend_at_war_timer
		}
		any_friend = {
			war = yes
			is_ruler = yes
			prisoner = no
			OR = {
				is_primary_war_attacker = yes
				is_primary_war_defender = yes
			}
			NOT = { trait = dragon }
		}
		NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 120
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = charitable
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = greedy
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = friend_at_war_timer
			duration = 1095
			hidden = yes
		}
		random_friend = {
			limit = {
				war = yes
				is_ruler = yes
				prisoner = no
				OR = {
					is_primary_war_attacker = yes
					is_primary_war_defender = yes
				}
				NOT = { trait = dragon }
			}
			save_event_target_as = friend_war_target
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100150
		trigger = {
			event_target:friend_war_target = {
				NOT = { is_vassal_or_below = ROOT }
				NOT = { is_liege_or_above = ROOT }
			}
		}
		event_target:friend_war_target = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_primary_war_attacker = yes
				}
				ROOT = {
					join_attacker_wars = PREV
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_primary_war_defender = yes
				}
				ROOT = {
					join_defender_wars = PREV
				}
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_very_grateful
				who = ROOT
				years = 5
			}
			letter_event = {
				id = 100151
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100151
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB100150
		event_target:friend_war_target = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_grateful
				who = ROOT
				years = 5
			}
			tooltip = {
				ROOT = {
					transfer_scaled_wealth = {
						to = PREV
						value = 0.25
					}
				}
			}
			letter_event = {
				id = 100152
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100152
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC100150
		random = {
			chance = 10
			event_target:friend_war_target = {
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_disappointed
					who = ROOT
					years = 5
				}
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 100153
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

					is_primary_war_defender = yes
				}
			}
			join_defender_wars = FROM
		}
		FROM = {
			set_character_flag = friend_joined_war
			character_event = {
				id = 100163
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100163
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC100162
		FROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = 100164
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100164
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = EVTDESC100163
	picture = GFX_evt_large_army
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100163 #Joined the war!
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = friend_joined_war
		}
		clr_character_flag = friend_joined_war
		tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_primary_war_attacker = yes
				}
				FROM = {
					join_attacker_wars = ROOT
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_primary_war_defender = yes
				}
				FROM = {
					join_defender_wars = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		opinion = {
			modifier = opinion_very_grateful
			who = FROM
			years = 5
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB100163
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_character_flag = friend_joined_war
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			transfer_scaled_wealth = {
				to = ROOT
				value = 0.25
			}
		}
		opinion = {
			modifier = opinion_grateful
			who = FROM
			years = 5
		}
	}

### My friend's friend is my friend ###
character_event = {
	id = friends_rivals.232

	is_triggered_only = yes
	capable_only = yes	
	hide_window = yes	
	min_age = 16
	prisoner = no
	war = no
	friends = yes
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		NOT = { num_of_friends = 5 }
		any_friend = {
			num_of_friends = 2
			prisoner = no
			NOT = { trait = dragon }		
			any_friend = {
				prisoner = no
				war = no
				OR = {
					at_location = ROOT
					is_liege_of = ROOT
					same_liege = ROOT
					vassal_of = ROOT
				}
				NOT = { num_of_friends = 5 }
				NOT = { character = ROOT }
				NOT = { is_close_relative = ROOT }
				NOT = { is_friend = ROOT }
				NOT = { is_rival = ROOT }
				NOT = { trait = dragon }
			}
		}	
		NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = trusting
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cruel
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = paranoid
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_friend = {
			limit = {
				num_of_friends = 2
				prisoner = no
				NOT = { trait = dragon }		
				any_friend = {
					prisoner = no
					war = no
					OR = {
						at_location = ROOT
						is_liege_of = ROOT
						same_liege = ROOT
						vassal_of = ROOT
					}
					NOT = { num_of_friends = 5 }
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					NOT = { is_close_relative = ROOT }
					NOT = { is_friend = ROOT }
					NOT = { is_rival = ROOT }
					NOT = { trait = dragon }
				}
			}	
			save_event_target_as = original_friend
			random_friend = {
				limit = {
					prisoner = no
					war = no
					OR = {
						at_location = ROOT
						is_liege_of = ROOT
						same_liege = ROOT
						vassal_of = ROOT
					}
					NOT = { num_of_friends = 5 }
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					NOT = { is_close_relative = ROOT }
					NOT = { is_friend = ROOT }
					NOT = { is_rival = ROOT }
					NOT = { trait = dragon }
				}
				character_event = { id = friends_rivals.233 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}

	id = friends_rivals.233

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROM = { character_event = { id = 100170 } }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = 100170
	desc = EVTDESC100170
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100170
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = gregarious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = kind
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = trusting
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				opinion = { who = FROM value = 25 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				opinion = { who = FROM value = 75 }
			}
		}
		event_target:original_friend = {
			character_event = {
				id = 100171
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100171
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = 100172
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100172
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB100170
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				trait = gregarious
				opinion = { who = FROM value = 25 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = shy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = cruel
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = paranoid
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -25 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -75 } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = gregarious
				opinion = { who = FROM value = 25 }
			}
			remove_trait = gregarious
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					personality_traits = 5
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = content
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = ambitious
				}
			}
			add_trait = content
		}		
		FROM = {
			set_character_flag = nofriends_friend
			character_event = {
				id = 100173
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100173
			}
		}
		event_target:original_friend = {
			character_event = {
				id = 100171
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100171
			}
		}
	}
}

### My friend is a much better diplomat than me, ask for help? ###
character_event = {
	id = 100190
	desc = EVTDESC100190
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	min_age = 16
	capable_only = yes
	war = no
	friends = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_abroad = no
		NOT = { diplomacy = 10 }
		NOT = { has_job_title = job_chancellor }
		NOT = {
			has_character_modifier = friend_diplomacy_timer
		}
		NOT = { trait = dragon }
		any_friend = {
			war = no
			prisoner = no
			diplomacy = 11
			NOT = { trait = dragon }
			NOT = { has_job_title = job_chancellor }
		}	
		NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }		
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			OR = {
				has_focus = focus_carousing
				has_ambition = obj_improve_diplomacy
			}
		}

			factor = 2
			trait = honest
		}

			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = trusting
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cruel
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = paranoid
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {

				hidden = yes
			}
		}
	}

		name = EVTOPTA100190
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10

				factor = 3
				trait = gregarious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = trusting
			}
		}

			limit = {
				war = no
				prisoner = no
				diplomacy = 11
				NOT = { trait = dragon }
			}
			character_event = {
				id = 100191
				days = 2

			}
		}
	}

		ai_chance = {

				NOT = {
					personality_traits = 5
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = ambitious
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = content
				}
			}
			add_trait = ambitious

#ROOT only gets help from friend if friend is paid
character_event = {
	id = 100194
	desc = EVTDESC100194
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100194
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				trait = greedy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				is_ruler = yes
				NOT = { scaled_wealth = 0.5 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				is_ruler = no
				NOT = { wealth = 15 }
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = 100195
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPA100195
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB100194
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}		
		change_diplomacy = 1
		tooltip = {
			transfer_scaled_wealth = {
				to = FROM
				value = 0.25
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_ruler = no }
			wealth = -15
		}
		FROM = {
			set_character_flag = paid_diplomacy
			character_event = {
				id = 100195
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPB100195
			}
		}
	}
}

#Friend is/n't paid by ROOT
character_event = {
	id = 100195
	desc = EVTDESC100195
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100195
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_character_flag = paid_diplomacy
			}
		}
		reverse_opinion = {
			modifier = opinion_disappointed
			who = FROM
			years = 5
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB100195
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = paid_diplomacy
		}
		clr_character_flag = paid_diplomacy
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_ruler = yes }
				transfer_scaled_wealth = {
					to = ROOT
					value = 0.25
				}
			}	
			if = {
				limit = { is_ruler = no }
				ROOT = { wealth = 15 }
			}
		}
	}
}

### My friend has much better martial stats than me, ask for help? ###
character_event = {
	id = 100200
	desc = EVTDESC100200
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	min_age = 16
	capable_only = yes
	war = no
	friends = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			is_female = no
			culture = kayakayanayan
			culture = samyrianan
			culture = bayasabhadi
		}
		NOT = { martial = 10 }
		NOT = { has_job_title = job_marshal }
		NOT = {
			has_character_modifier = friend_martial_timer
		}
		NOT = { trait = brilliant_strategist }
		NOT = { trait = dragon }
		any_friend = {
			war = no
			in_command = no
			OR = {
				is_female = no
				culture = kayakayanayan
				culture = samyrianan
				culture = bayasabhadi
			}
			prisoner = no
			martial = 11
			NOT = { has_job_title = job_marshal }
			NOT = { trait = misguided_warrior }
			NOT = { trait = dragon }
		}	
		NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }		
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			OR = {
				has_focus = focus_war
				has_ambition = obj_improve_martial
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = trusting
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cruel
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = paranoid
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_tooltip = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = friend_martial_timer
				duration = 1825
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100200
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = gregarious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = trusting
			}
		}
		random_friend = {
			limit = {
				war = no
				in_command = no
				OR = {
					is_female = no
					culture = kayakayanayan
					culture = samyrianan
					culture = bayasabhadi
				}
				prisoner = no
				martial = 11
				NOT = { has_job_title = job_marshal }
				NOT = { trait = misguided_warrior }
				NOT = { trait = dragon }
			}
			character_event = {
				id = 100201
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100201
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB100200
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = shy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = paranoid
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					personality_traits = 5
				}
				trait = diligent
				NOT = {
					trait = ambitious
				}
				NOT = { trait = content }
			}
			add_trait = ambitious
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					personality_traits = 5
				}
				trait = ambitious
				NOT = {
					trait = diligent
				}
				NOT = { trait = slothful }
			}
			add_trait = diligent
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = diligent
				trait = ambitious
			}
			prestige = 10
		}
	}
}

### My friend has much better stewardship stats than me, ask for help? ###
character_event = {
	id = 100210
	desc = EVTDESC100210
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	min_age = 16
	capable_only = yes
	war = no
	friends = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_abroad = no
		NOT = { stewardship = 10 }
		OR = {
			is_ruler = yes
			is_councillor = yes
			is_voter = yes
		}
		NOT = {
			has_character_modifier = friend_stewardship_timer
		}
		NOT = { trait = dragon }
		any_friend = {
			war = no
			prisoner = no
			stewardship = 11
			OR = {
				is_ruler = yes
				is_councillor = yes
				is_voter = yes
			}
			NOT = { trait = dragon }
		}	
		NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }		
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			OR = {
				has_focus = focus_rulership
				has_ambition = obj_improve_stewardship
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = trusting
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cruel
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = paranoid
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_tooltip = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = friend_stewardship_timer
				duration = 1825
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100210
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = gregarious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = trusting
			}
		}
		random_friend = {
			limit = {
				war = no
				prisoner = no
				stewardship = 11
				OR = {
					is_ruler = yes
					is_councillor = yes
					is_voter = yes
				}
				NOT = { trait = dragon }
			}
			character_event = {
				id = 100211
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100211
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB100210
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = shy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = paranoid
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					personality_traits = 5
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = ambitious
				}
				NOT = { trait = content }
			}
			add_trait = ambitious
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					personality_traits = 5
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = diligent
				}
				NOT = { trait = slothful }
			}
			add_trait = diligent
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						trait = diligent
						trait = ambitious
					}
					personality_traits = 5
				}
			}
			prestige = 10
		}
	}
}

#ROOT only gets help from friend if friend is paid
character_event = {
	id = 100214
	desc = EVTDESC100214
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100214
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				trait = greedy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				is_ruler = yes
				NOT = { scaled_wealth = 0.5 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				is_ruler = no
				NOT = { wealth = 15 }
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = 100215
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPA100215
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB100214
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				scaled_wealth = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.01
				NOT = {
					scaled_wealth = 0.5
				}
			}
		}		
		tooltip = {
			transfer_scaled_wealth = {
				to = FROM
				value = 0.25
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_ruler = no }
			wealth = -15
		}
		change_stewardship = 1
		location = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = friendly_innovations
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			set_character_flag = paid_stewardship
			character_event = {
				id = 100215
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPB100215
			}
		}
	}
}

#Friend is/n't paid by ROOT
character_event = {
	id = 100215
	desc = EVTDESC100215
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100215
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_character_flag = paid_stewardship
			}
		}
		tooltip = {
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_disappointed
				who = FROM
				years = 5
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB100215
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = paid_stewardship
		}
		clr_character_flag = paid_stewardship
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_ruler = yes }
				transfer_scaled_wealth = {
					to = ROOT
					value = 0.25
				}
			}	
			if = {
				limit = { is_ruler = no }
				ROOT = { wealth = 15 }
			}
		}
	}
}

### My friend has much better intrigue stats than me, ask for help? ###
character_event = {
	id = 100220
	desc = EVTDESC100220
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	min_age = 16
	capable_only = yes
	war = no
	friends = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_abroad = no
		NOT = { intrigue = 10 }
		NOT = {
			has_character_modifier = friend_intrigue_timer
		}
		NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
		NOT_mythical_creature_trigger = yes
		any_friend = {
			war = no
			prisoner = no
			intrigue = 11
			NOT = { trait = dragon }
		}		
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			OR = {
				has_focus = focus_intrigue
				has_ambition = obj_improve_intrigue
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = trusting
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cruel
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = paranoid
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_tooltip = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = friend_intrigue_timer
				duration = 1825
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100220
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = gregarious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = trusting
			}
		}
		random_friend = {
			limit = {
				war = no
				prisoner = no
				intrigue = 11
				NOT = { trait = dragon }
			}
			character_event = {
				id = 100221
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100221
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB100220
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = shy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = paranoid
			}
		}
		prestige = 10
		random = {
			chance = 10
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_dlc = "Reapers"
					}
				}
				add_trait = ill
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38290
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "Reapers"
				}
				add_symptom_effect = yes
			}		
		}
	}
}

### My friend has much better learning stats than me, ask for help? ###
character_event = {
	id = 100230
	desc = EVTDESC100230
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	min_age = 16
	capable_only = yes
	war = no
	friends = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOR = {
			religion = drowned_god
			religion = dothraki_pagan
		}
		NOT = {
			learning = 10
		}
		NOT = {
			has_character_modifier = friend_learning_timer
		}
		NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
		NOT = { trait = dragon }
		any_friend = {
			war = no
			prisoner = no
			learning = 11
			NOR = {
				religion = drowned_god
				religion = dothraki_pagan
			}
			OR = {
				piety = 100
				trait = zealous
			}
			religion = ROOT
			is_heretic = no
			NOT = { trait = dragon }
		}		
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			OR = {
				has_focus = focus_theology
				has_ambition = obj_improve_learning
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = trusting
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cruel
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = paranoid
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_tooltip = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = friend_learning_timer
				duration = 1825
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100230
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = gregarious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = trusting
			}
		}
		random_friend = {
			limit = {
				war = no
				prisoner = no
				learning = 11
				NOR = {
					religion = drowned_god
					religion = dothraki_pagan
				}
				OR = {
					piety = 100
					trait = zealous
				}
				religion = ROOT
				is_heretic = no
				NOT = { trait = dragon }
			}
			character_event = {
				id = 100231
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100231
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB100230
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = shy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = paranoid
			}
		}
		piety = 10
	}

### My friend is a hedonist ###
character_event = {
	id = 100250
	desc = EVTDESC100250
	picture = GFX_evt_feast
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	min_age = 23
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
	friends = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { lifestyle_traits = 1 }
		NOT = { has_character_flag = LE_ST }
		num_of_children = 2
		NOT = { trait = dragon }
		NOT = { trait = temperate }
		NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
		any_friend = {
			war = no
			prisoner = no
			trait = hedonist
			NOT = { trait = dragon }
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = chaste
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = lustful
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_friend = {
			limit = {
				war = no
				prisoner = no
				trait = hedonist
				NOT = { trait = dragon }
			}
			save_event_target_as = friend_100250
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100250
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				trait = lustful
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = gluttonous
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = gregarious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = trusting
			}
		}
		event_target:friend_100250 = {
			character_event = {
				id = 100251
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100251
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB100250
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				trait = chaste
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = rude
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.33
				trait = kind
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.33
				trait = patient
			}
		}
		event_target:friend_100250 = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_irritated
				who = ROOT
				years = 2
			}
			character_event = {
				id = 100252
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100252
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC100250
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				trait = chaste
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = shy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = paranoid
			}
		}
		prestige = 5
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = chaste
				NOR = {
					religion = drowned_god
					religion = dothraki_pagan
				}
			}
			add_trait = celibate
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = 100260
	desc = EVTDESC100260
	picture = GFX_evt_library
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes	
	min_age = 23
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	lacks_dlc = "Way of Life"
	war = no
	friends = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			lifestyle_traits = 1
		}
		NOT = {
			has_character_flag = LE_ST
		}
		NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
		num_of_children = 2
		NOT = { trait = dragon }
		any_friend = {
			war = no
			prisoner = no
			trait = scholar
			NOT = { trait = dragon }
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			learning = 15
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = content
		}
	}

		random_friend = {
			limit = {
				war = no
				prisoner = no
				trait = scholar

			}
			save_event_target_as = friend_100260

	}

				factor = 3

### I don't recognise my friend anymore, I don't know if we really are friends... ###
character_event = {
	id = 100350
	desc = EVTDESC100350
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking
	
	min_age = 16
	prisoner = no
	capable_only = yes
	friends = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { trait = dragon }
		NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
		any_friend = {
			NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_not_abandon_friendship } }
			OR = {
				NOT = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 } }
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_vengeance }
				any_current_enemy = { character = ROOT }
				AND = {
					trait = cruel
					ROOT = { NOT = { trait = cruel } }
				}
				AND = {
					trait = deceitful
					ROOT = { NOT = { trait = deceitful } }
				}
				AND = {
					trait = wroth
					ROOT = { NOT = { trait = wroth } }
				}
			}
			NOT = { trait = dragon }
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 500
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			any_friend = {
				NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_not_abandon_friendship } }
				OR = {
					NOT = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = -29 } }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_vengeance }
				}	
				NOT = { trait = dragon }
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = trusting
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = proud
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		#Try to find really bad friends first
		random_friend = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_not_abandon_friendship } }
				OR = {
					NOT = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = -29 } }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_vengeance }
				}
				NOT = { trait = dragon }
			}
			save_event_target_as = 100350_friend
			break = yes
		}
		random_friend = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_not_abandon_friendship } }
				OR = {
					NOT = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 } }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_vengeance }
					any_current_enemy = { character = ROOT }
					AND = {
						trait = cruel
						ROOT = { NOT = { trait = cruel } }
					}
					AND = {
						trait = deceitful
						ROOT = { NOT = { trait = deceitful } }
					}
					AND = {
						trait = wroth
						ROOT = { NOT = { trait = wroth } }
					}
				}
				NOT = { trait = dragon }
			}
			save_event_target_as = 100350_friend
		}
	}
	
	option = { #No longer friends
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 33
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				event_target:100350_friend = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_vengeance } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				event_target:100350_friend = { any_current_enemy = { character = ROOT } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				event_target:100350_friend = { NOT = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = -99 } } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				event_target:100350_friend = { NOT = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = -79 } } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				event_target:100350_friend = { NOT = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = -59 } } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				event_target:100350_friend = { NOT = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = -39 } } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				event_target:100350_friend = { NOT = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = -19 } } }
			}
			modifier = {

### My friend's rival tried to kill/maim/wound him/her! ###
character_event = {
	id = 100400
	desc = EVTDESC100400
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking
	
	min_age = 16
	prisoner = no
	capable_only = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	war = no
	friends = yes
	
	trigger = {
		combat_rating = 2
		OR = {
			is_female = no
			culture = kayakayanayan
			culture = samyrianan
			culture = bayasabhadi
		}
		NOT = { trait = dragon }
		NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
		any_friend = {
			war = no
			num_of_rivals = 1		
			OR = {
				is_female = no
				culture = kayakayanayan
				culture = samyrianan
				culture = bayasabhadi
			}
			prisoner = no
			NOT = { combat_rating = 5.17 }
			NOT = { trait = dragon }
			any_rival = {
				war = no
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = PREV modifier = attempted_murder }
				OR = {
					is_female = no
					culture = kayakayanayan
					culture = samyrianan
					culture = bayasabhadi
				}
				prisoner = no
				NOT = { is_friend = ROOT }
				NOT = { is_rival = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_friend = {
			limit = {
				war = no
				num_of_rivals = 1		
				OR = {
					is_female = no
					culture = kayakayanayan

					culture = bayasabhadi
				}
				prisoner = no
				NOT = { combat_rating = 5.17 }

			}

				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = honorable
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = just
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = brave
			}
		}
		event_target:rival_100400 = {
			tooltip = {

				years = 10
			}

			}

### I ask permission to challenge my rival into a duel ###

character_event = {
	id = friends_rivals.410
	
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 60
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	rivals = yes
	hide_window = yes
	war = no
	
	trigger = {
		is_abroad = no
		independent = no
		OR = {
			is_female = no
			culture = kayakayanayan
			culture = samyrianan
			culture = bayasabhadi
			culture_group = dornish
			culture_group = free_folk
		}
		NOT = { religion = nath_pagan }
		NOT = { has_severe_disability_trigger = yes }
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				is_ill = yes
				has_epidemic = yes
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_focus = focus_war }
		
		NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
		NOT = { trait = slave }
		
		is_priest = no
		NOT = { trait = silent_sister }
		NOT = { trait = maester }
		NOT = { trait = archmaester }
		NOT = { trait = septon }
		NOT = { trait = septa }
		NOT = { trait = silent_sister }
		NOT = { trait = red_priest }
		NOT = { trait = grace }	
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = recent_duel_timer }
		
		NOT = { trait = craven }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 500
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = duelist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = lunatic
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = wroth
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = patient
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_rival = {
			limit = {
				is_adult = yes
				same_liege = ROOT
				NOT = { is_liege_of = ROOT }
				NOT = { trait = slave }
				prisoner = no		
				NOT = { has_severe_disability_trigger = yes }	
				war = no			
				is_abroad = no
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						is_ill = yes
						has_epidemic = yes
					}
				}
				OR = { ### Not female or challenger religion accepts female warriors
					is_female = no
					ROOT = {
						OR = {
							culture = kayakayanayan
							culture = samyrianan
							culture = bayasabhadi
						}
					}
				} ### Not priest or challenger religion is pagan
				is_priest = no
				NOT = { trait = silent_sister }
				NOT = { trait = maester }
				NOT = { trait = archmaester }
				NOT = { trait = septon }
				NOT = { trait = septa }
				NOT = { trait = silent_sister }
				NOT = { trait = red_priest }
				NOT = { trait = grace }	
				NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
				
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = duel_rival
				}
				
				NOT = { has_character_modifier = recent_duel_timer }			
				NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_fought_duel } }
				NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_fought_duel } }
				NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_fled_duel } }
			}	
			save_event_target_as = duel_rival
			ROOT = { character_event = { id = 100410 } }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}

				event_target:duel_rival = { trait = skilled_warrior }

					OR = {

					}
				}

				NOT = { trait = lunatic }
			}
		}

			clr_character_flag = duel_rival
			character_event = {
				id = 100415
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100415
			}
		}
	}
	option = {

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					trait = brave
					is_strong_trigger = yes
					trait = master_warrior

#Cheating rival attempts to clear his name
character_event = {
	id = 100423
	desc = EVTDESC100423
	picture = GFX_evt_joust
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100423
		trigger = { diplomacy = 10 }
		tooltip_info = diplomacy
		random_opinion_modifier_target = {
			limit = {
				is_ruler = yes
				OR = {
					has_character_flag = melee_begins
					has_character_flag = tournament_begins
				}	
				OR = {			
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_attending_tournament }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_spectating_tournament }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_attending_melee }
				}
				OR = {			
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = PREV modifier = opinion_attending_tournament }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = PREV modifier = opinion_spectating_tournament }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = PREV modifier = opinion_attending_melee }
				}
			}
			any_opinion_modifier_target = {
				limit = {
					has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_disgraceful }
					prisoner = no
					NOT = { character = PREVPREV }
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					OR = {
						has_character_flag = attending_tournament
						has_character_flag = attending_archery_tournament
						has_character_flag = attending_melee
					}
					OR = {			
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = PREV modifier = opinion_attending_tournament }
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = PREV modifier = opinion_spectating_tournament }
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = PREV modifier = opinion_attending_melee }
					}
					OR = {
						trait = trusting
						opinion = { who = ROOT value = -15 }
					}
				}
				remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_disgraceful }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trait = trusting
						opinion = { who = ROOT value = -15 }
					}
				}
				remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_disgraceful }
			}	
		}
		reverse_opinion = {
			modifier = opinion_disgraceful
			who = FROM
			years = 10
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB100423
		prestige = -40
		reverse_opinion = {
			modifier = opinion_disgraceful
			who = FROM
			years = 10
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = 100427
	desc = EVTDESC100427
	picture = GFX_evt_melee
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100427
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = poor_warrior
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = trained_warrior
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 6
				trait = skilled_warrior
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 8
				trait = master_warrior
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 6
				trait = duelist
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 8
				trait = brave
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				is_strong_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = tall
			}
			#Avoid fights
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_severe_disability_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				trait = wounded
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.05
				trait = craven
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				religion = nath_pagan
			}
			modifier = {
				religion = the_seven
				is_priest = yes
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				is_female = no
				FROM = { is_female = yes }
				factor = 0.025
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { 
			FROM = {
				set_character_flag = flag_duel_friendly
				set_character_flag = friends_rivals_duel
				add_character_modifier = {
					modifier = recent_duel_timer
					duration = 365
					hidden = yes
				}
			}
			set_character_flag = flag_duel_friendly
			set_character_flag = friends_rivals_duel
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = recent_duel_timer
				duration = 365
				hidden = yes
			}
			e_rebels = { holder_scope = { character_event = { id = duel.0 } } } #duel engine
		} 
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB100427
		trigger = { NOT = { trait = berserker } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				FROM = { trait = poor_warrior }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				FROM = { trait = trained_warrior }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				FROM = { trait = skilled_warrior }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				FROM = { trait = master_warrior }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				FROM = { is_strong_trigger = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				FROM = { trait = tall }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 6
				trait = craven
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = paranoid
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				is_weak_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = dwarf
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = hunchback
			}
		}
		prestige = -25
		reverse_opinion = {
			modifier = opinion_coward
			who = FROM
			years = 10
		}
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = 100429
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100429
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					personality_traits = 5
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = craven
				}
				NOT = { trait = brave }
			}
			add_trait = craven
		}
	}
}

### Make your liege distrust your rival ###
character_event = {
	id = 100450
	desc = EVTDESC100450
	picture = GFX_evt_throne_room
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	only_rulers = yes
	min_age = 16
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
	rivals = yes
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		independent = no
		NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
		any_rival = {
			war = no
			age = 16
			same_sex = ROOT
			in_command = no
			same_liege = ROOT
			prisoner = no
			liege = {
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
				opinion = { who = ROOT value = 10 }
				opinion = { who = PREV value = 10 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = wroth
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = honest
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOTPA100450
		random_rival = {
			limit = {
				war = no
				age = 16
				same_sex = ROOT
				in_command = no
				same_liege = ROOT
				prisoner = no
				liege = {
					NOT = {
						character = ROOT
					}
					opinion = { who = ROOT value = 10 }
					opinion = { who = PREV value = 10 }
				}
			}
			set_character_flag = devious_rival
			liege = {
				character_event = {
					id = 100451
					tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100451
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOTPB100450
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					personality_traits = 6
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = honest
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = deceitful
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 10
				add_trait = honest
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38262 #Notify Honest
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					personality_traits = 6
				}
				trait = honest
				NOT = {
					trait = content
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = ambitious
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 10
				add_trait = content
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38279 #Notify Content
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						trait = honest
						trait = content
					}
					personality_traits = 6
				}
			}
			prestige = 10
		}
	}
}

#Liege listens to you
character_event = {
	id = 100451
	desc = EVTDESC100451
	picture = GFX_evt_throne_room
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOTPA100451
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.01
				trait = gregarious
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			random_rival = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = devious_rival
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_friend = ROOT
					}
					remove_friend = ROOT
				}
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_grateful
				who = ROOT
				years = 5
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				set_character_flag = liege_believes
				character_event = {
					id = 100452
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOTPB100451
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = gregarious
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			random_rival = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = devious_rival
				}
				clr_character_flag = devious_rival
			}
			character_event = {
				id = 100452
				days = 1
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100452
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = 100460
	desc = EVTDESC100460
	picture = GFX_evt_scandal
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	min_age = 16
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
	rivals = yes
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
		any_rival = {
			war = no
			age = 16
			in_command = no

### A rival of yours is so much beneath you that it seems a bit silly of you to hold him as an enemy ###	
character_event = {
	id = 100470
	desc = EVTDESC100470
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	only_rulers = yes
	min_age = 16
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
	rivals = yes
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		NOT = {
			has_character_modifier = recalculate_rivalry_modifier
		}
		any_rival = {
			war = no
			age = 16
			in_command = no
			prisoner = no
			same_sex = ROOT
			lower_tier_than = ROOT
			NOT = { is_close_relative = ROOT }
			NOT = { father_even_if_dead = { NOT = { lower_tier_than = ROOT } } }
			NOT = { mother_even_if_dead = { NOT = { lower_tier_than = ROOT } } }
			NOT = { any_claim = { NOT = { lower_tier_than = ROOT } } }
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_tooltip = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = recalculate_rivalry_modifier
				duration = 1825
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
		random_rival = {
			limit = {
				war = no
				age = 16
				in_command = no
				prisoner = no
				same_sex = ROOT
				lower_tier_than = ROOT
				NOT = { is_close_relative = ROOT }
				NOT = { father_even_if_dead = { NOT = { lower_tier_than = ROOT } } }
				NOT = { mother_even_if_dead = { NOT = { lower_tier_than = ROOT } } }
				NOT = { any_claim = { NOT = { lower_tier_than = ROOT } } }
			}
			save_event_target_as = recalculate_rivalry
		}	
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100470
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = ruthless
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = stubborn
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				event_target:recalculate_rivalry = { just_execution_reason_PREV_trigger = yes }
			}
		}
		event_target:recalculate_rivalry = {
			remove_rival = ROOT
			if = {
				limit = {
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_revenge_seeker }
				}
				reverse_remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_revenge_seeker }
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				character_event = {
					id = 100471
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB100470
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = patient
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = honorable
			}
		}
		prestige = 10
	}
}

### You have been made aware that your fierce rival is planning rebellious acts ###
character_event = {
	id = 100490
	desc = EVTDESC100490
	picture = GFX_evt_council
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	only_rulers = yes
	min_age = 16
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
	rivals = yes
	
	trigger = {	
		in_command = no
		independent = no
		is_plot_active = no
		NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
		any_rival = {
			war = no
			age = 16
			in_command = no
			prisoner = no
			is_plot_active = no
			is_ruler = yes
			same_liege = ROOT
			NOT = { intrigue = ROOT }
			plot_target_char = {
				NOT = { character = ROOT }
				is_liege_of = ROOT
			}		
			OR = {
				has_plot = plot_gain_liege_title
				has_plot = plot_instigate_revolt
				has_plot = plot_kidnap_liege
				has_plot = plot_fabricate_treason_liege
				has_plot = plot_seize_trade_post
				has_plot = plot_investigate_legitimacy
				has_plot = plot_replace_regent
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100490
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = honest
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = patient
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { personality_traits = 6 }
				NOT = { trait = ambitious }
				NOT = { trait = content }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 10		
				add_trait = ambitious
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38278 #Notify Ambitious
					}
				}
			}
		}	
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { personality_traits = 6 }
				NOT = { trait = ambitious }
				NOT = { trait = diligent }
				NOT = { trait = slothful }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 10		
				add_trait = diligent
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38256 #Notify diligent
					}
				}
			}
		}	
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { intrigue = 10 }
			}
			change_intrigue = 1				
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB100490
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				trait = honorable
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				liege = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = ruthless
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = deceitful
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = wroth
			}
		}
		random_rival = {
			limit = {
				war = no
				age = 16
				in_command = no
				prisoner = no
				is_plot_active = no
				is_ruler = yes
				same_liege = ROOT
				NOT = { intrigue = ROOT }
				plot_target_char = {
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					is_liege_of = ROOT
				}		
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_gain_liege_title
					has_plot = plot_instigate_revolt
					has_plot = plot_kidnap_liege
					has_plot = plot_fabricate_treason_liege
					has_plot = plot_seize_trade_post
					has_plot = plot_investigate_legitimacy
					has_plot = plot_replace_regent
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				back_plot = PREV
			}
			character_event = {
				id = 100491
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100491
			}
		}
	}
}
