### Root tries to wound rival during hunt ###
character_event = {
	id = 100510
	desc = EVTDESC100510
	picture = GFX_evt_hunt
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	rivals = yes
	
	trigger = {
		any_rival = {
			OR = {
				character = FROM
				AND = {
					same_liege = PREV
					at_location = PREV
				}
			}		
			combat_rating = 2
			age = 16
			OR = {
				is_female = no
				culture = kayakayanayan
				culture = samyrianan
				culture = bayasabhadi
			}
			in_command = no
			NOT = { trait = dragon }
			prisoner = no
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			is_adult = yes
			NOT = {	health_traits = 1 }
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_tooltip = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = hunting_rival_timer
				duration = 2000
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
		random_rival = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					character = FROM
					AND = {
						same_liege = PREV
						at_location = PREV
					}
				}		
				combat_rating = 2
				age = 16
				OR = {
					is_female = no
					culture = kayakayanayan
					culture = samyrianan
					culture = bayasabhadi
				}
				in_command = no
				NOT = { trait = dragon }
				prisoner = no
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				is_adult = yes
				NOT = {	health_traits = 1 }
			}
			save_event_target_as = hunting_rival
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100510
		event_target:hunting_rival = {
			hidden_tooltip = {
				character_event = {
					id = 100511
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				65 = {
					
				}
				20 = {
					add_trait = wounded
				}
				10 = {
					add_maimed_trait_effect = yes
				}
				5 = {
					set_character_flag = rival_killed_me
					tooltip = {
						death = {
							death_reason = death_accident
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}	
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC100510
		random = {
			chance = 10
			character_event = {
				id = 36010
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP36010
			}
		}
	}
}

### Poison rival during liege's feast ###
character_event = {
	id = 100520
	desc = EVTDESC100520
	picture = GFX_evt_feast
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	min_age = 16
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
	rivals = yes
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no		
		NOT = {
			has_character_modifier = master_poisoner
		}
		NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
		any_rival = {
			same_liege = ROOT
			age = 16
			OR = {
				has_character_flag = guest_feast_started
				has_character_flag = coming_to_feast
				is_ruler = no
			}
			in_command = no
			prisoner = no
			NOT = { intrigue = ROOT }
			NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
		}
		liege = {
			has_character_flag = host_feast_started
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100520
		random_rival = {
			limit = {
				same_liege = ROOT
				age = 16
				OR = {
					has_character_flag = guest_feast_started
					has_character_flag = coming_to_feast
					is_ruler = no
				}
				in_command = no
				prisoner = no
				NOT = { intrigue = ROOT }
				NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
			}
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						ROOT = {
							character_event = {
								id = 100521
							}
						}
					}
				}
				20 = {
					tooltip = { add_trait = ill }
					set_character_flag = poisoned_ill
					hidden_tooltip = {
						character_event = {
							id = 100522
						}
					}
				}
				15 = {
					tooltip = { add_trait = infirm }
					set_character_flag = poisoned_infirm
					hidden_tooltip = {
						character_event = {
							id = 100522
						}
					}
				}
				10 = {
					tooltip = { 
						death = {
							death_reason = death_murder_unknown
						}
					}
					set_character_flag = poisoned_killed
					hidden_tooltip = {
						character_event = {
							id = 100522
						}
					}
				}
				5 = {
					liege = {
						tooltip = { add_trait = ill }
						character_event = {
							id = 100523
							tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100523
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB100520
	}
}

#Liege is poisoned
character_event = {
	id = 100523
	desc = EVTDESC100523
	picture = GFX_evt_feast
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100523
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_dlc = "Reapers" } }
			add_trait = ill
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "Reapers" }
			set_character_flag = disease_not_serious
			add_trait = vomiting
			character_event = { id = RIP.11005 days = 10 random = 30 }
		}	
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { num_of_vassals = 2 }
			}
			random_vassal = {
				limit = {
					age = 40
					has_character_flag = guest_feast_started
					NOT = { character = FROM }
					ai = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_dlc = "Reapers" } }
					add_trait = ill
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_dlc = "Reapers" }
					set_character_flag = disease_not_serious
					add_trait = vomiting
					character_event = { id = RIP.11005 days = 10 random = 30 }
				}
				set_character_flag = poisoned_at_feast
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { num_of_vassals = 3 }
			}
			random_vassal = {
				limit = {
					age = 16
					trait = drunkard
					has_character_flag = guest_feast_started
					NOT = { character = FROM }
					ai = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_dlc = "Reapers" } }
					add_trait = ill
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_dlc = "Reapers" }
					set_character_flag = disease_not_serious
					add_trait = vomiting
					character_event = { id = RIP.11005 days = 10 random = 30 }
				}
				set_character_flag = poisoned_at_feast
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				num_of_vassals = 4
			}
			random_vassal = {
				limit = {
					age = 16
					trait = gluttonous
					has_character_flag = guest_feast_started
					NOT = { character = FROM }
					ai = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_dlc = "Reapers" } }
					add_trait = ill
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_dlc = "Reapers" }
					set_character_flag = disease_not_serious
					add_trait = vomiting
					character_event = { id = RIP.11005 days = 10 random = 30 }
				}
				set_character_flag = poisoned_at_feast
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					intrigue = FROM
					job_spymaster = {
						intrigue = FROM
					}
				}
			}
			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = guest_feast_started
					NOT = { character = FROM }
				}
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_poisoner
					who = ROOT
					years = 5
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					intrigue = FROM
					job_spymaster = {
						intrigue = FROM
					}
				}
			}
			tooltip = {
				FROM = {
					character_event = {
						id = 100525
						tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100525
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				character_event = {
					id = 100525
					tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100525
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### Revenge seeker seeks revenge ###
character_event = {
	id = 100530
	desc = EVTDESC100530
	picture = GFX_evt_council
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	min_age = 16
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
	rivals = yes
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = revenge_seeker_timer }
		NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
		any_rival = {
			war = no
			in_command = no
			prisoner = no
			OR = {
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_vengeance }
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_revenge_seeker }
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_tooltip = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = revenge_seeker_timer
				duration = 1825
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
		random_rival = {
			limit = {
				war = no
				in_command = no
				prisoner = no
				OR = {
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_vengeance }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_revenge_seeker }
				}				
			}	
			save_event_target_as = revenge_seeker_target
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100530 #Rumours
		trigger = {
			is_ruler = yes
			event_target:revenge_seeker_target = {
				is_ruler = yes
			}
		}
		event_target:revenge_seeker_target = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					any_vassal = {
						opinion = {
							modifier = opinion_lost_respect
							who = PREV
							years = 5
						}
					}
					character_event = {
						id = 100531
						tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100531
					}
				}
				50 = {
					ROOT = {
						character_event = {
							id = 100532
							tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100532
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB100530 #Kill
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		event_target:revenge_seeker_target = {
			character_event = {
				id = 100533
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100533
			}			
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC100530 #Maim/wound
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				is_maimed_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				trait = wounded
			}
		}
		event_target:revenge_seeker_target = {
			character_event = {
				id = 100534
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100534
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTD100530 #Ignore
		event_target:revenge_seeker_target = {
			if = {
				limit = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_revenge_seeker } }
				reverse_remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_revenge_seeker }
			}	
		}
	}
}

		any_vassal = {

				modifier = opinion_lost_respect
				who = ROOT
				years = 5
			}
		}
		prestige = -10
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					intrigue = FROM
					job_spymaster = {
						intrigue = FROM
					}
				}
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_revenge_seeker
				who = FROM
				years = 100
			}
			FROM = {
				set_character_flag = rival_discovered_slanderer
				tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 100537
						tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100537
					}
				}
			}
		}

				character_event = {
					id = 100537
				}
			}
		}
	}

#ROOT tried to kill Rival
character_event = {
	id = 100535
	desc = EVTDESC100535
	picture = GFX_evt_spymaster
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100535
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = revenge_killer
			NOT = {
				has_character_flag = revenge_maim
			}
			NOT = {
				has_character_flag = revenge_wound
			}
		}
		clr_character_flag = revenge_killer
		remove_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_revenge_seeker }
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = hot_revenge
			duration = 1825
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB100535
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_character_flag = revenge_killer
			}
			NOT = {
				has_character_flag = revenge_maim
			}
			NOT = {
				has_character_flag = revenge_wound
			}
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = poor_revenge_seeker
			duration = 365
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC100535
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = revenge_wound
			NOT = {
				has_character_flag = revenge_killer
			}
			NOT = {
				has_character_flag = revenge_maim
			}
		}
		clr_character_flag = revenge_wound
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = hot_revenge
			duration = 730
		}
		remove_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_revenge_seeker }
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTD100535
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = revenge_maim
			NOT = {
				has_character_flag = revenge_killer
			}
			NOT = {
				has_character_flag = revenge_wound
			}
		}
		clr_character_flag = revenge_maim
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = hot_revenge
			duration = 1095
		}

	}
}

### Son seeks revenge for his father ###
character_event = {
	id = 100540
	desc = EVTDESC100540
	picture = GFX_evt_council
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
	rivals = yes
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		NOT = {
			has_character_modifier = killed_father_timer
		}
		NOT = {
			has_character_flag = avenged_father
		}
		NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
		any_rival = {
			war = no
			in_command = no
			prisoner = no
			reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_vengeance }
			ROOT = { 
				father_even_if_dead = { 
					death_reason = death_murder
					killer = { character = PREVPREVPREV } 
				} 
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_tooltip = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = killed_father_timer
				duration = 1825
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
		random_rival = {
			limit = {
				war = no
				in_command = no
				prisoner = no
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_vengeance }
				ROOT = { 
					father_even_if_dead = { 
						death_reason = death_murder
						killer = { character = PREVPREVPREV } 
					} 
				}
			}
			save_event_target_as = father_killer
		}	
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100540 #Rumours
		trigger = {
			event_target:father_killer = {
				is_ruler = yes
			}
		}
		event_target:father_killer = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					any_vassal = {
						opinion = {
							modifier = evil_murderer
							who = PREV
							years = 5
						}
					}
					character_event = {
						id = 100541
						days = 7
						random = 7
						tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100541
					}
				}
				50 = {
					ROOT = {
						character_event = {
							id = 100542
							days = 7
							random = 7
							tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100532
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB100540 #Kill
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				is_maimed_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				trait = wounded
			}
		}
		event_target:father_killer = {
			character_event = {
				id = 100543
				days = 7
				random = 7
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100543
			}			
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC100540 #Maim/wound
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				is_maimed_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				trait = wounded
			}
		}
		event_target:father_killer = {
			character_event = {
				id = 100544
				days = 7
				random = 7
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP100544
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTD100540 #Ignore
	}
}

#ROOT: Father's Murderer got away/is killed
character_event = {
	id = 100545
	desc = EVTDESC100545
	picture = GFX_evt_spymaster
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA100545
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = revenge_killer
			NOT = {
				has_character_flag = revenge_maim
			}
			NOT = {
				has_character_flag = revenge_wound
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = avenged_father
		clr_character_flag = revenge_killer
		remove_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_revenge_seeker }
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = hot_revenge
			duration = 1825
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB100545
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_character_flag = revenge_killer
			}
			NOT = {
				has_character_flag = revenge_maim
			}
			NOT = {
				has_character_flag = revenge_wound
			}
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = poor_revenge_seeker
			duration = 365
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC100545
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = revenge_wound
			NOT = {
				has_character_flag = revenge_killer
			}
			NOT = {
				has_character_flag = revenge_maim
			}
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = hot_revenge
			duration = 730
		}
		clr_character_flag = revenge_wound
		set_character_flag = avenged_father
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTD100545
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = revenge_maim
			NOT = {
				has_character_flag = revenge_killer
			}
			NOT = {
				has_character_flag = revenge_wound
			}
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = hot_revenge
			duration = 1095
		}
		clr_character_flag = revenge_maim
		set_character_flag = avenged_father
	}
}

### My friend could make a good guardian ###
character_event = {
	id = friends_rivals.1
	desc = EVTDESCfriends_rivals.1
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	only_rulers = yes	
	min_age = 16
	prisoner = no
	capable_only = yes	
	ai = yes #player can freely choose guardian
	friends = yes
	
	trigger = {		
		any_child = {
			age = 6
			NOT = { age = 14 }
			is_ruler = no
			liege = { character = ROOT }
			is_alive = yes
			NOT = { trait = bastard }
			prisoner = no
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			NOT = { educator = { is_friend = ROOT } }
			NOT = { educator = { ai = no } } #do not confuse player
			NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
			NOT = { has_character_modifier = guardian_friend_found } #stops repeated requests if AI overrides
		}
		any_friend = {
			is_ruler = yes
			age = 16
			prisoner = no
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			NOT = { trait = dragon }
			NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
			NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
		}
		NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }		
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 24
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = paranoid
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_child = {
			limit = {
				age = 6
				NOT = { age = 14 }
				is_ruler = no
				liege = { character = ROOT }
				is_alive = yes
				NOT = { trait = bastard }
				prisoner = no
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				NOT = { educator = { is_friend = ROOT } }
				NOT = { educator = { ai = no } } #do not confuse player
				NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
				NOT = { has_character_modifier = guardian_friend_found } #stops repeated requests if AI overrides
			}
			save_event_target_as = potential_ward
		}
		random_friend = {
			limit = {
				is_ruler = yes
				age = 16
				prisoner = no
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				NOT = { trait = dragon }
				NOT = {
					any_ward = {
						is_alive = yes
						count = 2
					}
				}
				NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
				NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
				NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_refused_guardianship } }
			}
			save_event_target_as = potential_guardian
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = YES
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = { #Ill-suited for martial education
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					event_target:potential_ward = { has_character_modifier = martial_education }
					event_target:potential_ward = { has_focus = focus_ed_martial }
				}
				event_target:potential_guardian = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							martial = 10
							trait = skilled_warrior
							trait = master_warrior
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = { #Ill-suited for steward education
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					event_target:potential_ward = { has_character_modifier = steward_education }
					event_target:potential_ward = { has_focus = focus_ed_stewardship }
				}
				event_target:potential_guardian = {
					NOT = { stewardship = 10 }
				}
			}
			modifier = { #Wrong culture
				factor = 0
				event_target:potential_guardian = {
					NOT = { culture_group = ROOT }
				}
				OR = {
					trait = proud
					trait = paranoid
					trait = wroth
				}
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { name = high_valyrian_cull value = off }
					AND = {
						NOT = { culture = high_valyrian }
						NOT = { culture = western_valyrian }
						NOT = { culture = eastern_valyrian }	
					}
				}				
			}
			modifier = { #Wrong religion
				factor = 0
				event_target:potential_guardian = {
					NOT = { religion = ROOT }
				}
				trait = zealous		
			}
			modifier = { #Idiot
				factor = 0
				event_target:potential_guardian = {
					NOT = { higher_tier_than = ROOT }
					NOT = { learning = 7 }
					NOT = { stewardship = 7 }
					NOT = { diplomacy = 7 }
					NOT = { intrigue = 7 }
					NOT = { martial = 7 }
				}	
			}
		}
		event_target:potential_guardian = { letter_event = { id = friends_rivals.2 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = NO
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0.1
		}
		clear_event_target = potential_ward
		clear_event_target = potential_guardian
	}
}

letter_event = {
	id = friends_rivals.2
	desc = EVTDESCfriends_rivals.2
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = OPTAfriends_rivals.2 #Yes
		event_target:potential_ward = {
			set_guardian = ROOT
			hidden_tooltip = {
				add_character_modifier = { #stops repeated requests if AI overrides
					name = guardian_friend_found
					duration = 1825
					hidden = yes
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			opinion = {
				who = FROM
				modifier = opinion_entrusted_ward
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = OPTBfriends_rivals.2 #No
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		FROM = {
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = opinion_refused_guardianship
			}
		}
	}
}
### Rivalry between heir and step-parent ###
character_event = {
	id = friends_rivals.5
	desc = EVTDESCfriends_rivals.5
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion

	is_triggered_only = yes
	min_age = 16
	capable_only = yes
	only_playable = yes
	hide_window = yes
	
	trigger = {		
		current_heir = {
			age = 16
			is_liege_or_above = ROOT
			is_child_of = ROOT
			prisoner = no
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			ROOT = {
				any_spouse = {
					is_alive = yes
					age = 16
					is_liege_or_above = ROOT
					prisoner = no
					NOT = { trait = incapable }
					NOT = { any_child = { character = PREVPREVPREV } }
					NOT = { is_rival = PREVPREV }
					NOT = { is_friend = PREVPREV }
					NOT = { opinion = { who = PREVPREV value = 0 } }
					NOT = { reverse_opinion = { who = PREVPREV value = 25 } }
					any_child = {
						is_alive = yes
						is_female = no
						is_child_of = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}		
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		current_heir = {
			ROOT = {
				random_spouse = {
					limit = {
						is_alive = yes
						age = 16
						is_liege_or_above = ROOT
						prisoner = no
						NOT = { trait = incapable }
						NOT = { any_child = { character = PREVPREVPREV } }
						NOT = { is_rival = PREVPREV }
						NOT = { is_friend = PREVPREV }
						NOT = { opinion = { who = PREVPREV value = 0 } }
						NOT = { reverse_opinion = { who = PREVPREV value = 25 } }
						any_child = {
							is_alive = yes
							is_female = no
							is_child_of = ROOT
						}
					}
					character_event = { id = friends_rivals.6 }
				}
			}
		}		
	}
	
	option = {
		name = OK					
	}
}
character_event = { #Spouse decides
	id = friends_rivals.6
	desc = EVTDESCfriends_rivals.6
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAfriends_rivals.6
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				FROM = { current_heir = { NOT = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = -20 } } } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				FROM = { current_heir = { NOT = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = -40 } } } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				FROM = { current_heir = { NOT = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = -60 } } } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				FROM = { current_heir = { NOT = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = -80 } } } }
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = greedy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = envious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = arbitrary
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = familyperson
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = ambitious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = cruel
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = ruthless
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = wroth
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = friends_rivals.7 } }
			current_heir = {
				add_rival = ROOT
				hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = friends_rivals.8 } }
				any_sibling = {
					limit = { 
						is_alive = yes
						OR = {
							mother_even_if_dead = {
								NOT = { character = ROOT_FROM }
								any_child = { character = PREVPREVPREV }
							}
							father_even_if_dead = {
								NOT = { character = ROOT_FROM }
								any_child = { character = PREVPREVPREV }
							}
						}
						NOT = { opinion = { who = ROOT value = 20 } }
						NOT = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 20 } }
						NOT = { is_friend = ROOT }
					}
					add_rival = ROOT
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = friends_rivals.9 } }
				}
				ROOT = {
					any_child = {
						limit = { 
							is_alive = yes
							NOT = { opinion = { who = PREVPREV value = 20 } }
							NOT = { reverse_opinion = { who = PREVPREV value = 20 } }
							NOT = { is_friend = PREVPREV }
						}
						add_rival = PREVPREV
						hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = friends_rivals.10 } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBfriends_rivals.6
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = charitable
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = honest
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = just
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = slothful
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = content
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = kind
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = honorable
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = patient
			}
		}
	}
}

						NOT = { is_friend = PREVPREV }

				}
			}
		}
	}

character_event = { #Inform Spouse's Children
	id = friends_rivals.10
	desc = EVTDESCfriends_rivals.10
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAfriends_rivals.10
		FROMFROM = { 
			current_heir = { 
				add_rival = ROOT 
				any_sibling = {
					limit = { 
						is_alive = yes
						OR = {
							mother_even_if_dead = {
								NOT = { character = ROOT_FROMFROM }
								any_child = { character = PREVPREVPREV }
							}
							father_even_if_dead = {
								NOT = { character = ROOT_FROMFROM }
								any_child = { character = PREVPREVPREV }
							}
						}
						NOT = { opinion = { who = ROOT value = 20 } }
						NOT = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 20 } }
						NOT = { is_friend = ROOT }
					}
					add_rival = ROOT
				}
			} 
		}
	}
}
